 if (newWindow)
 window.open(url, '_blank');
 else
 document.location = url;
 }

 function runOnLoad(fn) { loadQueue.push(fn); }
 window.onload = function() {
 for (var i = 0; i < loadQueue.length; i++)
 loadQueue[i]();
 delete loadQueue;
 };

  /** Converts a <button> to look like an <a> tag. */
  .linkify {
    display: inline;
    padding: 0;
    margin: 0;
    border: 0;
    background: 0;
    cursor: pointer;
  }
  h1, h2, h3, h4 {
    background: none;

  a, chops-button, a.button, .button, .linkify {
    color: var(--chops-link-color);
    text-decoration: none;
    font-weight: var(--chops-link-font-weight);
    font-family: var(--chops-font-family);
  }
  a:hover, .linkify:hover {
    text-decoration: underline;
  }
  a.button, .button {
    /* Links that look like buttons. */
    display: inline-flex;
    align-items: center;
    justify-content: center;
    text-decoration: none;
    transition: filter 0.3s ease-in-out, box-shadow 0.3s ease-in-out;
  }
  a.button:hover, .button:hover {
    filter: brightness(95%);

  }

    display: block;
    margin-right: 4px;
  }
  chops-button.emphasized, a.button.emphasized, .button.emphasized {
    background: var(--chops-primary-button-bg);

  }
  textarea, select, input {
    box-sizing: border-box;
    font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
  }
  /* Note: decoupling heading levels from styles is useful for
  * accessibility because styles will not always line up with semantically
  * appropriate heading levels.

  .medium-heading {

          --monorail-metadata-toggled-bg: var(--monorail-metadata-closed-bg);
        }
        mr-issue-page[codeFont] {
          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;

        }

          width: 100%;

          flex-wrap: no-wrap;
        }

        }

          flex-grow: 0;

          overflow-y: auto;

          height: calc(100vh - var(--monorail-header-height));
        }

            width: 100%;

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

<br>





# Use-after-Free on HandleOnPerformDrop



<span class="line"><!----># Use-after-Free on HandleOnPerformDrop<!----></span>



<br>





## Root Cause and some notes



<span class="line"><!---->## Root Cause and some notes<!----></span>



<br>





[0] The `web_contents` is posted to a separate sequence



<span class="line"><!---->[0] The `web_contents` is posted to a separate sequence<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[1] `web_contents` may be destroyed in UI by the time the it runs, causing a UAF in ScanData callback.



<span class="line"><!---->[1] `web_contents` may be destroyed in UI by the time the it runs, causing a UAF in ScanData callback.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/3041006



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/3041006"><!---->https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/3041006<!----></a>



<br>





The pattern of this vulnerability is similar to this patch.



<span class="line"><!---->The pattern of this vulnerability is similar to this patch.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<br>



<br>





[2] The root cause of this vulnerability is very clear, but to quick trigger this vulnerability, we need to patch two codes.



<span class="line"><!---->[2] The root cause of this vulnerability is very clear, but to quick trigger this vulnerability, we need to patch two codes.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





- First add `sleep(3)` at the beginning of the GetPathsToScan function. **Note that we can block the thread pool or create a folder, which continuously recursively stores the recursive folder to achieve the effect of sleep(3) , Because the for loop in GetPathsToScan needs to recursively scan and obtain some file information, which will take some time, so this patch is not necessary**



<span class="line"><!---->- First add `sleep(3)` at the beginning of the GetPathsToScan function. **Note that we can block the thread pool or create a folder, which continuously recursively stores the recursive folder to achieve the effect of sleep(3) , Because the for loop in GetPathsToScan needs to recursively scan and obtain some file information, which will take some time, so this patch is not necessary**<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





```cpp



<span class="line"><!---->```cpp<!----></span>



<br>





enterprise_connectors::ContentAnalysisDelegate::Data GetPathsToScan(



<span class="line"><!---->enterprise_connectors::ContentAnalysisDelegate::Data GetPathsToScan(<!----></span>



<br>





    content::WebContents* web_contents,



<span class="line"><!---->    content::WebContents* web_contents,<!----></span>



<br>





    const content::DropData& drop_data,



<span class="line"><!---->    const content::DropData&amp; drop_data,<!----></span>



<br>





    enterprise_connectors::ContentAnalysisDelegate::Data data) {



<span class="line"><!---->    enterprise_connectors::ContentAnalysisDelegate::Data data) {<!----></span>



<br>





  sleep(3);//add sleep to here



<span class="line"><!---->  sleep(3);//add sleep to here<!----></span>



<br>





  for (const auto& file : drop_data.filenames) {



<span class="line"><!---->  for (const auto&amp; file : drop_data.filenames) {<!----></span>



<br>





    base::File::Info info;



<span class="line"><!---->    base::File::Info info;<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





    // Ignore the path if it's a symbolic link.



<span class="line"><!---->    // Ignore the path if it's a symbolic link.<!----></span>



<br>





    if (!base::GetFileInfo(file.path, &info) || info.is_symbolic_link)



<span class="line"><!---->    if (!base::GetFileInfo(file.path, &amp;info) || info.is_symbolic_link)<!----></span>



<br>





      continue;



<span class="line"><!---->      continue;<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





    // If the file is a directory, recursively add the files it holds to |data|.



<span class="line"><!---->    // If the file is a directory, recursively add the files it holds to |data|.<!----></span>



<br>





    if (info.is_directory) {



<span class="line"><!---->    if (info.is_directory) {<!----></span>



<br>





      base::FileEnumerator file_enumerator(file.path, /*recursive=*/true,



<span class="line"><!---->      base::FileEnumerator file_enumerator(file.path, /*recursive=*/true,<!----></span>

## Reproduce



<span class="line"><!---->## Reproduce<!----></span>



<br>





1. Refer to the instructions for simple patching of the code



<span class="line"><!---->1. Refer to the instructions for simple patching of the code<!----></span>



<br>





2. Start chrome with the following parameters.



<span class="line"><!---->2. Start chrome with the following parameters.<!----></span>



<br>





3. Before the second page is closed by `window.close`, drag a non-empty folder to the page.



<span class="line"><!---->3. Before the second page is closed by `window.close`, drag a non-empty folder to the page.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>





python3 -m http.server 8000



<span class="line"><!---->python3 -m http.server 8000<!----></span>



<br>





out/release/chrome "about:blank" 127.0.0.1:8000/test.html



<span class="line"><!---->out/release/chrome "about:blank" 127.0.0.1:8000/test.html<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->  Array cookie:            ac<!----></span>

  Intra object redzone:    bb



<span class="line"><!---->  Intra object redzone:    bb<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->  ASan internal:           fe<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->  Left alloca redzone:     ca<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->  Right alloca redzone:    cb<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->  Shadow gap:              cc<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->==47272==ABORTING<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>

#### Please briefly explain who can exploit the vulnerability, and what they gain when doing so



<span class="line"><!---->#### Please briefly explain who can exploit the vulnerability, and what they gain when doing so<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This vulnerability can be used for sandbox escape, because the vulnerability is in the browser process, not in the render.



<span class="line"><!---->This vulnerability can be used for sandbox escape, because the vulnerability is in the browser process, not in the render.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Because `enterprise_connectors::ContentAnalysisDelegate::IsEnabled`,so enterprise users are more vulnerable to attacks.



<span class="line"><!---->Because `enterprise_connectors::ContentAnalysisDelegate::IsEnabled`,so enterprise users are more vulnerable to attacks.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





As long as the user is induced to drag the malicious folder to the malicious page, it may trigger a stable sandbox escape.



<span class="line"><!---->As long as the user is induced to drag the malicious folder to the malicious page, it may trigger a stable sandbox escape.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<br>





Before a merge request will be considered, the following information is required to be added to this bug:



<span class="line"><!---->Before a merge request will be considered, the following information is required to be added to this bug:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





1. Does your merge fit within the Merge Decision Guidelines?



<span class="line"><!---->1. Does your merge fit within the Merge Decision Guidelines?<!----></span>



<br>





- Chrome: 



<span class="line"><!---->- Chrome: <!----></span>





https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src.git/+/main/docs/process/merge_request.md#when-to-request-a-merge



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src.git/+/main/docs/process/merge_request.md#when-to-request-a-merge"><!---->https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src.git/+/main/docs/process/merge_request.md#when-to-request-a-merge<!----></a>



<br>





- Chrome OS: 



<span class="line"><!---->- Chrome OS: <!----></span>





https://goto.google.com/cros-release-branch-merge-guidelines



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://goto.google.com/cros-release-branch-merge-guidelines"><!---->https://goto.google.com/cros-release-branch-merge-guidelines<!----></a>



<br>





2. Links to the CLs you are requesting to merge.



<span class="line"><!---->2. Links to the CLs you are requesting to merge.<!----></span>



<br>





3. Has the change landed and been verified on ToT?



<span class="line"><!---->3. Has the change landed and been verified on ToT?<!----></span>



<br>





4. Does this change need to be merged into other active release branches (M-1, M+1)?



<span class="line"><!---->4. Does this change need to be merged into other active release branches (M-1, M+1)?<!----></span>



<br>





5. Why are these changes required in this milestone after branch?



<span class="line"><!---->5. Why are these changes required in this milestone after branch?<!----></span>



<br>





6. Is this a new feature?



<span class="line"><!---->6. Is this a new feature?<!----></span>



<br>





7. If it is a new feature, is it behind a flag using finch?



<span class="line"><!---->7. If it is a new feature, is it behind a flag using finch?<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Chrome OS Only:



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome OS Only:<!----></span>



<br>





8. Was the change reviewed and approved by the Eng Prod Representative? See Eng Prod ownership by component: 



<span class="line"><!---->8. Was the change reviewed and approved by the Eng Prod Representative? See Eng Prod ownership by component: <!----></span>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.



<span class="line"><!---->Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.<!----></span>
